[2;36m                    [0m         [35m/tmp/[0m[95mtmpt8trbq9i[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[95mtestcase[0m[39m -t ghcr.io/aixcc-finals/base-runner:v1.[0m[1;36m3.0[0m[39m reproduce [0m    [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m===Evaluation [0m[33mReport[0m[39m===[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m# Evaluation Report[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Summary[0m                                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mA heap-use-after-free vulnerability has been detected in the Wireshark telnet [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdissector [0m[1;39m([0m[39m`packet-telnet.c`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m during fuzzing operations. The issue occurs when [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mattempting to write [0m[1;36m4[0m[39m bytes to a memory region that has already been freed. The [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mvulnerability is triggered during the processing of telnet protocol data, [0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mspecifically in the `telnet_add_text` function when it attempts to access memory [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mthat was previously freed in `telnet_sub_option`.[0m                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Description[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe issue manifests as an AddressSanitizer heap-use-after-free error with a [0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mseverity score of [0m[1;36m46[0m[39m [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m4[0m[39m-byte-write-heap-use-after-free[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m. The vulnerability occurs [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mduring the dissection of telnet packets in the Wireshark protocol analyzer.[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Key observations from the stack trace:**[0m                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Write Location**: The invalid write occurs in `telnet_add_text` at [0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[35m/src/wireshark/epan/dissectors/[0m[95mpacket-telnet.c[0m[39m:[0m[1;36m2211[0m[39m`, which calls [0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`tvb_get_raw_bytes_as_stringz`, subsequently calling `tvb_memcpy`, and ultimately [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`memcpy` where the actual memory access violation happens.[0m                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Memory Allocation**: The problematic memory region [0m[1;39m([0m[1;36m1920[0m[39m bytes at address [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m0x51c000000880[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m was originally allocated in `dissect_naws_subopt` at line [0m[1;36m652[0m[39m of [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`packet-telnet.c` through a `g_malloc` call.[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Memory Deallocation**: The same memory region was freed in `telnet_sub_option`[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mat line [0m[1;36m2099[0m[39m of `packet-telnet.c` through `wmem_simple_free`.[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Execution Flow**: The vulnerability is triggered during the following [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msequence:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `dissect_telnet` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2322[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m calls `telnet_command` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2182[0m[1;39m)[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `telnet_command` calls `telnet_sub_option` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2099[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which frees the memory[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Control returns to `dissect_telnet` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2337[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m which then calls [0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`telnet_add_text` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2211[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `telnet_add_text` attempts to access the already-freed memory[0m                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Vulnerability Type**: Heap-use-after-free [0m[1;39m([0m[39mUse-After-Free[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m - a temporal memory [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39msafety violation where memory is accessed after it has been deallocated.[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m**Test Case**: The fuzzer input that triggers this vulnerability consists of:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m\[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m372[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m037[0m[39m\000P\[0m[1;36m000[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m030[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m360[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m372[0m[39m\"\[0m[1;36m001[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m001[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m\360aaaa[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mexamined:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m     - `tvb_memcpy` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m945[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                      [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m18[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m* One of the supposed benefits of wmem over the old emem was going to be that[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m19[0m[39m: * the scoping of the various memory pools would be obvious, since they would[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m20[0m[39m: * no longer be global. Instead, the pools would be managed as variables scoped[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m21[0m[39m: * by the compiler, so functions outside of that scope wouldn't have access to[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m22[0m[39m: * the pools and wouldn't be able to allocate memory in a scope to which they[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m23[0m[39m: * didn't belong.[0m                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m24[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m25[0m[39m: * That idea fell apart rather quickly :P[0m                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m26[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m27[0m[39m: * The principle still stands, and most pools should be managed in that way.[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m28[0m[39m: * The three in this file are *exceptions*. They are the three scopes that emem[0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m29[0m[39m: * provided as globals. Converting all of the code that used them to pass an[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m30[0m[39m: * extra parameter [0m[1;39m([0m[39mor three[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m around would have been a nightmare of epic[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m31[0m[39m: * proportions, so we provide these three as globals still.[0m                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m32[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m33[0m[39m: * We do, however, use some extra booleans and a mountain of assertions to try[0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m34[0m[39m: * and catch anybody accessing the pools out of the correct scope. It's not[0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m35[0m[39m: * perfect, but it should stop most of the bad behaviour that emem permitted.[0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m36[0m[39m: *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m37[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m38[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m* TODO: Make these thread-local *[0m[35m/[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m39[0m[39m:static wmem_allocator_t *packet_scope;[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m40[0m[39m:static wmem_allocator_t *file_scope;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m41[0m[39m:static wmem_allocator_t *epan_scope;[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m42[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m43[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m* Packet Scope *[0m[35m/[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m44[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m45[0m[39m:wmem_allocator_t *[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m46[0m[39m:[0m[1;35mwmem_packet_scope[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m47[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m48[0m[39m:    [0m[1;35mws_assert[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket_scope[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m49[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m50[0m[39m:    return packet_scope;[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m51[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m52[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m53[0m[39m:void[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m54[0m[39m:[0m[1;35mwmem_enter_packet_scope[0m[1;39m([0m[39mvoid[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m55[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m{[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<code>[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mepan/packet_info.h:[0m[1;36m150[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m178[0m                                                          [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m158[0m[39m:  int dissection_depth;         [0m[35m/[0m[39m**< The current [0m[32m"depth"[0m[39m or layer number in the[0m [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m161[0m[39m:[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m packet_info;[0m                                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m162[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m163[0m[39m:[0m[35m/[0m[39m** @[0m[1;39m}[0m[39m *[0m[35m/[0m                                                                       [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m165[0m[39m:#endif [0m[35m/[0m[39m* __PACKET_INFO_H__ *[0m[35m/[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m166[0m[39m:[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m175[0m[39m: *[0m                                                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m176[0m[39m: * ex: set [0m[33mshiftwidth[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m [0m[33mtabstop[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m expandtab:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m177[0m[39m: * :[0m[33mindentSize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m2[0m[39m:[0m[33mtabSize[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m8[0m[39m:[0m[33mnoTabs[0m[39m=[0m[35mtrue[0m[39m:[0m                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode[0m[39m>[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mcode_snippets[0m[39m>[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<fix_strategy>[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Analysis of the Issue[0m                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAfter analyzing the evaluation report and the relevant code snippets, I've [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39midentified the root cause of the heap-use-after-free vulnerability in the Wireshark[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtelnet dissector:[0m                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Root Cause[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe NAWS [0m[1;39m([0m[39mNegotiate About Window Size[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m implementation has a fundamental memory [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmanagement flaw:[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Global variables storing packet-scoped memory** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m70[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m72[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m94[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - `hf_telnet_width`, `hf_telnet_height`, `hf_telnet_line`, `hf_naws_data` are [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatic global variables[0m                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - These persist across all packet dissections[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Incorrect memory allocation scope** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m652[0m[39m in `dissect_naws_subopt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Allocates `hf_naws_data` from `pinfo->pool` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket-scoped memory[0m[1;39m)[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Stores this pointer in a global variable that outlives the packet[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Premature memory deallocation** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m640[0m[39m in `dissect_linemode_subopt`[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - When a LINEMODE suboption is processed, it explicitly frees `hf_naws_data`[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - However, the flag `hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set` remains set to [0m[1;36m1[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Use-after-free in telnet_add_text** [0m[1;39m([0m[39mline [0m[1;36m2211[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m:[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Checks `hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set` flag [0m[1;39m([0m[39mstill [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m after linemode freed the [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbuffer[0m[1;39m)[0m                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - Attempts to write to the freed `hf_naws_data` buffer[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Execution Flow with Fuzzer Input[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fuzzer input `\[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m372[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m037[0m[39m\000P\[0m[1;36m000[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m030[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m360[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m372[0m[39m\"\[0m[1;36m001[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m001[0m[39m\[0m[1;36m377[0m[39m\360aaaa` [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtriggers:[0m                                                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. First NAWS suboption: allocates [0m[1;36m80[0m[39m×[0m[1;36m24[0m[39m=[0m[1;36m1920[0m[39m bytes into `hf_naws_data`[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. Second LINEMODE suboption: frees `hf_naws_data` but leaves flag set[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. Regular data [0m[32m"aaaa"[0m[39m: `telnet_add_text` tries to use freed `hf_naws_data`[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Fix Strategy[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe proper fix requires migrating from global state to per-connection state stored [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39min the conversation data structure, following the existing `telnet_conv_info_t` [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpattern.[0m                                                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m1[0m[39m: Extend the Conversation Data Structure[0m                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mModify the `telnet_conv_info_t` structure [0m[1;39m([0m[39maround line [0m[1;36m232[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m236[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to include [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNAWS-related state:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mtypedef struct _telnet_conv_info [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uint32_t  starttls_requested_in;[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uint32_t  starttls_port;[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    ssize_t   vmotion_sequence_len;[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Add NAWS state members:[0m                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uint16_t  naws_width;          [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Terminal width in columns[0m                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uint16_t  naws_height;         [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Terminal height in rows[0m                       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uint16_t  naws_line;           [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Current line number [0m[1;39m([0m[39mfor wrapping[0m[1;39m)[0m            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    uint8_t  *naws_data;           [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Window buffer data[0m                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    bool      naws_enabled;        [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Whether NAWS is currently active[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m[39m telnet_conv_info_t;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m2[0m[39m: Remove Global Variables[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRemove the global state variables [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m70[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m72[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m94[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m that are causing the issue:[0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remove: `static int hf_telnet_width;`[0m                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remove: `static int hf_telnet_height;`[0m                                            [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remove: `static int hf_telnet_line;`[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- Remove: `static uint8_t *hf_naws_data;`[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mNote: Do NOT remove `static int hf_telnet_naws_subopt_set;` if it's used as a [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mprotocol field handle for display purposes. However, the flag functionality should [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmove to the conversation structure.[0m                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Step [0m[1;36m3[0m[39m: Modify dissect_naws_subopt Function[0m                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mRewrite `dissect_naws_subopt` [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m645[0m[39m-[0m[1;36m662[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to use conversation data and [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mfile-scoped memory:[0m                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```c[0m                                                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatic void[0m                                                                         [2m                [0m

[2;36m                    [0m         [39mstatic telnet_conv_info_t *[0m                                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;35mtelnet_get_session[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpacket_info *pinfo[0m[1;39m)[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m{[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  conversation_t        *conversation = [0m[1;35mfind_or_create_conversation[0m[1;39m([0m[39mpinfo[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  telnet_conv_info_t    *telnet_info;[0m                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  telnet_info = [0m[1;39m([0m[39mtelnet_conv_info_t*[0m[1;39m)[0m[1;35mconversation_get_proto_data[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconversation, [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mproto_telnet[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                                                                      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  if [0m[1;39m([0m[39m!telnet_info[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m [0m[1;39m{[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    telnet_info = [0m[1;35mwmem_new0[0m[1;39m([0m[1;35mwmem_file_scope[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, telnet_conv_info_t[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    telnet_info->vmotion_sequence_len = [0m[1;36m-1[0m[39m;[0m                                         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[35m/[0m[35m/[0m[39m Initialize NAWS fields [0m[1;39m([0m[39mwmem_new0 already zeros them, but be explicit[0m[1;39m)[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    telnet_info->naws_data = NULL;[0m                                                  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    telnet_info->naws_enabled = false;[0m                                              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    telnet_info->naws_width = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    telnet_info->naws_height = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    telnet_info->naws_line = [0m[1;36m0[0m[39m;[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m    [0m[1;35mconversation_add_proto_data[0m[1;39m([0m[39mconversation, proto_telnet, telnet_info[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m;[0m           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  [0m[1;39m}[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m  return telnet_info;[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m}[0m                                                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m```[0m                                                                                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m## Justification[0m                                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Why This is the Optimal Approach[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Follows Wireshark Best Practices**: Uses the conversation API pattern already [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mestablished in the codebase for `starttls_requested_in` and `vmotion_sequence_len`.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Correct Memory Scope**: Allocates from `[0m[1;35mwmem_file_scope[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` instead of [0m         [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`pinfo->pool`, ensuring the buffer persists across packet dissections.[0m              [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Per-Connection State**: Stores state in the conversation structure, allowing [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mmultiple telnet connections to be tracked independently without interference.[0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Automatic Memory Management**: wmem automatically frees file-scoped memory [0m    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwhen the capture file is closed, preventing memory leaks.[0m                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m5[0m[39m. **Preserves Existing Logic**: The NAWS functionality remains intact - terminal [0m  [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwindow buffering still works as intended by RFC [0m[1;36m1184[0m[39m.[0m                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### How It Addresses the Issues[0m                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Eliminates Use-After-Free**: Memory is no longer freed prematurely during [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mpacket dissection; it persists for the entire conversation lifetime.[0m                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Removes Global State**: No more race conditions or interference between [0m       [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdifferent connections or packets.[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Proper Lifecycle Management**: The linemode dissector can still disable NAWS, [0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mbut now it properly clears all state in the conversation structure.[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m4[0m[39m. **Bounds Checking**: Added validation to prevent excessive memory allocations [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;39m([0m[39mmax [0m[1;36m1024[0m[39m×[0m[1;36m1024[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m and buffer overruns.[0m                                                [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Potential Side Effects and Mitigation[0m                                           [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m1[0m[39m. **Memory Usage**: Per-connection buffers may increase memory usage if many large[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mterminal windows are negotiated.[0m                                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Added bounds checking [0m[1;39m([0m[39mmax [0m[1;36m1024[0m[39m×[0m[1;36m1024[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m to prevent abuse.[0m        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m2[0m[39m. **Function Signature Change**: `telnet_add_text` now requires `pinfo` parameter.[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Only two call sites need updating [0m[1;39m([0m[39mlines [0m[1;36m2317[0m[39m, [0m[1;36m2337[0m[1;39m)[0m[39m, both are[0m [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mwithin the same file.[0m                                                               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [1;36m3[0m[39m. **Conversation Tracking**: Requires proper conversation identification.[0m          [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m   - **Mitigation**: Already handled by existing `[0m[1;35mfind_or_create_conversation[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` [0m   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39minfrastructure.[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m### Similar Solutions in Codebase[0m                                                   [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mThe fix follows the exact same pattern used for:[0m                                    [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- `starttls_requested_in` and `starttls_port` in `telnet_conv_info_t`[0m               [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- TN3270 and TN5250 conversation tracking via `[0m[1;35mfind_tn3270_conversation[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m` and [0m     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m`[0m[1;35mfind_tn5250_conversation[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`[0m                                                        [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m- VMware vMotion sequence length tracking in `vmotion_sequence_len`[0m                 [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mAll of these use conversation-scoped data allocated from `[0m[1;35mwmem_file_scope[0m[1;39m([0m[1;39m)[0m[39m`, [0m      [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39mdemonstrating this is the established pattern for the telnet dissector.[0m             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m                                                                                             [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         [39m<[0m[35m/[0m[95mfix_strategy[0m[1m>[0m                                                                     [2m                [0m
[2;36m                    [0m         ===Evaluation [33mEnd[0m===                                                                [2m                [0m
